Free Talk

No Longer "Dissent" 192

— Zhishui

It's funny to say, after writing a bit of my own and submitting it to "Free Talk" for publication, I couldn't find my own piece. I didn't clip and save that day's "Free Talk". So today, after reading Mr. Huang Huaibai's "After Reading the Dissent on Creation and Time", I couldn't even pick out my own "dissent" to carefully examine it. But Mr. Huang's first article is still clipped in the pile of letters. Comparing the two, I am satisfied with Mr. Huang, because in this second article he has already said that he "never said that creation only needs sufficient time and can abandon other conditions."

Although rereading Mr. Huang's first article (September 17th "Creation and Time") carefully, one cannot help but say that the center of gravity of his argument is on the two words "time", and that he has ignored "other conditions", but now I am quite satisfied with Mr. Huang's argument in the second article.

However, Mr. Huang this time also said, "How can one only talk about 'life experience', 'observation' and 'thought' as Mr. Zhishui said, there are also 'imagination', 'emotion', and 'descriptive skills', etc., this can be appealed to 'common sense' to know". Well said, well said! Putting "imagination" and "emotion" on the list of "elements of creation" is quite old-fashioned "common sense". I don't quite trust such "common sense". I believe that "imagination" and "emotion" both start from "life experience". People with different "life experiences" often have different "imaginations" and "emotions", so it is not appropriate to put them together when discussing them. And I remember that I never put "life experience" and "observation" and "thought" together for discussion, as Mr. Huang quoted!

And I also don't understand why an article discussing "creation and time" would be called "digressing from the topic" if it mentioned life experience, etc.? Furthermore, because there are no good creations, "hoping that writers will not cherish time too much", and citing "historical examples" of completing a book in ten or twenty years, is it no wonder that people think the commentator is "limited to a rigid time relationship"? Therefore, I feel that my previous "dissent" was not a "purely arbitrary judgment". If Mr. Huang's first article had the same tone as his current second article, I would naturally not say that his views were limited to a rigid time relationship. Isn't this a very simple matter? Mr. Huang's first article did not imply anything about the relationship with life experience, my "dissent" raised the "relationship with life experience", so how can this be considered erasing other people's opinions?

This time, Mr. Huang also used Scott and Balzac, whom I cited in my "dissent", to explain that both of them were forced to overwork because of debt. It can be seen that Mr. Huang also admits that their creations did not have ten or twenty years of careful consideration. However, since Mr. Huang cannot deny that all their works are not great, then doesn't Mr. Huang's argument in the first article lightly overturn itself? Mr. Huang said in the first article that Goethe "spent a full fifty years" to complete "Faust", but this time he turned around and said "roughly so", and also said "at least eating, sleeping, reading, and talking must have taken up a part of his time", but in fact, during those "fifty years", Goethe was busy with other things besides "eating, sleeping, reading, and talking", so it's not enough to say "roughly so"; however, Mr. Huang also overturned his own argument in the first article. These are all reasons why I am satisfied with Mr. Huang's second article. I am deeply gratified that my "dissent" did not "erase other people's opinions".

A few final words: Mr. Huang also said in this article, "Zola's Rougon-Macquart series also took more than twenty years of effort to write"; this tone is somewhat similar to Mr. Huang's belief in "ten years, twenty years, fifty years" in his first article; but Zola's twenty years wrote a total of twenty volumes of books, each with about 200,000 words! Dividing it by the years, Zola is still not "cherishing time too much"! As for Mr. Huang's statement this time that "therefore, there are still people criticizing Scott's works for not having very real internal emotions and thoughts, and Zola also made the mistake of being lengthy in his descriptive techniques. Even these great writers inevitably have minor flaws due to their 'prolific' nature, which is even more conceivable for others." This passage is applied a little bit "out of bounds". Scott's "not very real" is because he did not use the techniques of realism, and Zola's "lengthy" is partly related to his naturalistic theory and partly because his "style" is like that, and cannot be considered a failure because of his "prolific" nature.

But the most interesting thing is that my "dissent" cited Scott and others who wrote a large book in one year to disagree with Mr. Huang's first article's examples of completing a book in ten years, twenty years, or fifty years. And this time, Mr. Huang conversely used the facts of Scott, etc., to "dare to say: Mr. Zhishui's cited honors of Scott, etc. in the literary world were all obtained through long-term efforts and hard work". In this way, people who only read Mr. Huang's second article will mistakenly think that I attribute the acquisition of Scott's and others' "honors" to not having gone through long-term efforts.

But in fact, my original statement is exactly Mr. Huang's current statement. However, Mr. Huang's first article only said that only by completing a book in ten years, twenty years, or even fifty years can it be great, while my "dissent" said that a writer who completes a book in one year can also be great, as long as his "life experience" is rich—and of course, he must also have literary cultivation. And the so-called "rich life experience" and "literary cultivation" are the so-called "long-term efforts". This "effort" cannot be rigidly estimated by the time spent writing a book.

If Mr. Huang did not have the idea of "abandoning other conditions" in mind when writing his first article, then the tone of his first article should be like his current second article, right? Furthermore, if he did distinguish the essential difference between "completing a book in twenty years or even fifty years" and Scott's and others' "long-term efforts and hard work" when writing his second article, then his second article might not be what it is now, right? But this is truly so-called "arbitrary judgment". Let's not say too much.

Countryside 193

— Yi

Living in the city, tired of hearing the noisy sounds of traffic, tired of seeing the grayness of walls and roofs, I always think of going to the countryside, but when I get to the countryside, especially the countryside with the feeling of autumn, it makes people unwilling to live there for a long time. A little rain turns the road into mud, making it difficult to set foot. Not to mention this, the sight of trees covered with old leaves in mixed yellow and green, shivering under the blowing of the cold wind, is enough to make people lose a lot of vitality.

Do you think you can still sit leisurely under that willow tree by the river, hugging your knees, and watch the white geese playing on the water for a while? But you always smell the scent of dog feces and the like in the half-yellow grass. When you go to a courtyard, the first thing you see is pieces of cloth stained with excrement and urine flying under the eaves. The cow tied to the tree in the courtyard may have been led away, but the cow dung and cow urine mixed with dry straw are still conspicuously left behind. When sitting on a short, squeaky stool, you have to be careful all the time that the bottom of your clothes doesn't sweep the dirty things that chickens have scattered on the ground. The dog that initially barked fiercely at you, after being scolded by its owner, tucks its tail and quiets down, and now comes over like a child and sniffs you with its nose, putting the chaff that it stole from the pig feed on your shoes.

"Come and see, is this house good?"

Following the owner in, the cobwebs hanging like tassels on the roof beams, covered with dust, have been swept away and can no longer be seen. You can barely live in it, but looking out from the windows made of a few branches, under the mulberry tree with leaves fluttering in the wind, there are two huge manure vats placed askew. Thinking about it, let's pull the clumsy wooden door on the window, which is slightly coated with a bit of yellow tung oil, to close it, but the room will be completely dark, and you need a Western candle to read. More particular families may have one or two pieces of glass tile installed on the low tile roof, but they are either gray and blurry, or a little dark yellow, and it is also not certain that there are three or five yellow leaves piled on top.

Who can go to the countryside near Shanghai to rent a farmhouse and not get such an impression?

However, the countryside seen from the car window, boat window, or horseback is good and full of poetry. However, if you do not have the determination and courage to "improve the countryside" or "go to the people", but just return to the countryside to eat old rice and live day by day, it is really unbearable for people who are used to walking on asphalt roads and using electric lights and running water. What's more, today's countryside is collapsing in a mess.

However, in the eyes of a farmer who lives in the countryside for a long time, there is no such gentlemanly disgust for the countryside. As long as there is no knocking on the door to collect taxes and rent, no conscription, and no endless wars, then even living in the same house with cattle and eating at a table with a chicken coop underneath is quite satisfactory. But in fact, they are forced to leave, forever leaving their familiar and lovely countryside. Now the countryside has become uninhabitable for the people of the countryside. How can intellectuals who love the countryside not hate it?

Therefore, people who want to "go to the people" today need as much courage as going to the battlefield.

Night Walk 194

— Zigang

Unintentionally, I slipped into the market far away from my residence before dusk. There, unintentionally, I picked up a few broken books with all the money I had at the book stall. When I walked out the door, I was met by a friend who looked like an old brother, and it was so unintentional!

As we talked, I was invited into a theater. Let the buried theater addiction open its eyes again.

After the crowd dispersed, I went to the parking lot to pick up my bicycle. There was no light on the bicycle. To avoid being out at night, I don't usually leave it on the bike.

"It's not okay without a light!"

"It's okay, the weather is clear, it's good if it doesn't rain. I'll buy another one after I pass by the bicycle shop." The ground is slightly damp, it's a road, and the ditches on both sides are flowing like small rivers while swallowing. This sound reminds me of the endless flowing water in front of my house in Jiangnan. Don't many people envy the small bridge and flowing water?

But now I am far away in my hometown across thousands of mountains and rivers!

"Let's go," I muttered to myself after seeing the well-meaning middle-aged man walk away. I touched my pocket, it was empty.

I walked closely to the left, like a thief in the middle of the night, trying to dodge the sight of the police. They would interfere, especially to save electricity and rickshaw fare. They are often harshly scolded to stop until they turn on the lights.

I stepped on the pedals hard, letting the bicycle glide quickly, my heart was beating slightly. There were so many police stations! There was a black uniform standing underneath.

Too bad he doesn't have eyes on all sides. I smiled secretly, seeing that I had escaped the first police station, the black uniform was facing away from me.

I borrowed the light from other bicycles along the way, following closely. As soon as I got to a police station, I slanted to the side, it was best to have the ability to be invisible! Raindrops leaked from the trees with dense leaves one after another on the side of the street, passing through my hair, my head was strangely cool, and my hands and sleeves were also full of cool drips.

"Turn on the lights, female cyclist, that female cyclist!" Finally, I was caught.

"Ignore him, the cat catches the mouse!" I silently glided past again.

I was shouted at again and again, and I was almost detained. I was defeated, okay, I surrender. I got off the bicycle and pushed it on the sidewalk. The big lamp in front of the Palace Museum was shining brightly. I haven't been there yet, it costs half a dollar to see the gate all the way. I only cared about looking around, and I kept stepping on mud pits under my feet. Water got into the seams of my leather shoes and soaked my feet. It was even more difficult when I entered the alley. People say that the alleys in Peiping are three feet of dust without wind, that may be a bit of a lie, but three inches of mud on rainy days is indeed true. Several times, my feet were as difficult to pull out as if they were stuck in a small pot. I arrived at the steps of my residence. My feet looked like pine blossoms covered with yellow soil.

In the small alley, the vendor selling hard noodles was shouting, his voice was so lonely. The basket on his back looked very heavy. On a rainy day, where would there be buyers? Thank you for his hand-held lamp, which illuminated the door knocker I was knocking on.

Little West Assistant 195

— By Langston Hughes, Translated by Fo Lang

(1)

In the reception room of the Overseas Merchants' Hotel, there were six large brass spittoons – one in each corner, one in the middle, and one placed near the registration clerk's desk. Xin Di's job was to clean these spittoons. Every winter evening, after school, he would run into the hotel through the back door, put his books in the cupboard where he kept his broom and rag, sweep the two small dining rooms, dust the stairs and the reception room, then take these spittoons and pour the viscous phlegm into the alley, rinse them with water, and polish them until they shone as if they were made of gold. Apart from the slight odor during cleaning, Xin Di rather liked this job. He often felt very proud that around six o'clock, he could see the six formerly phlegm-filled but now shining spittoons in the dirty old reception room, reflecting the electric lights, all done by his own hands and with the help of polishing oil to increase their shine, which never failed to please Xin Di.

He liked cleaning things, making them beautiful and shiny, just like his old grandmother, Hager: when she wasn't doing laundry, she would often sweep the house, wipe the stairs, or scrub the kitchen floor until it was clean enough. Granny Hager found cleaned things beautiful, and so did Xin Di. Every evening, he was proud of his six clean brass spittoons. Although every day when he came to work, they were refilled with tobacco juice, cigarette butts, gum residue, and phlegm, it was Xin Di's job to clean them – and when they were cleaned, they were beautiful again.

Cha Xiang Na Tuo was right: this job wasn't too difficult, and he liked that it only took a little time. He was interested and fascinated by the new life he saw in the hotel, but he was a quiet child by nature, and he didn't have many questions to ask. No one told him anything except his work supervisor. Xin Di swept well, and the head waiter never had a chance to scold him, because he was always scolding the two bellhop boys.

The Overseas Merchants' Hotel wasn't a large hotel, nor was it a refined one. It was a three-story building, already dilapidated and about to collapse, and hadn't been painted for many years. In the reception room, two large glass windows looked out onto the street, and in front of them were rows of hardwood chairs. At the back of the reception room was the registration clerk's desk, a box of cigars and cigarettes, a pot of cold water, and a door leading to the men's restroom, cleaning which was also Xin Di's responsibility.

Upstairs on the second and third floors were the bedrooms. Only very poor traveling salesmen and temporary railroad workers frequented them, and occasionally some performers, and street women and their patrons rented them. The Overseas Merchants' Hotel was often busiest in the evenings, but only on Saturdays. That night, Xin Di's work started after six o'clock and he couldn't go home until ten or eleven, but his grandmother Hager was always waiting for him, warming the fire and filling a bucket of water for his once-a-week bath.

Education News

Germany Reforms Education System 196

School lessons from Monday to Friday

Saturday for Hitler Youth training

National teachers study various issues

Teachers without achievements in cooperation groups will be disqualified

(Special dispatch from Beiping) According to German education expert Xisheng's interview with reporters, Sweden is the most outstanding example of a modern education system because it can use new methods to improve previous deficiencies in order to meet needs. Germany is now actively improving its education, and the educational policies it has set are attracting the attention of educators around the world and are considered to be of great value. The German education system involves a kind of competition between schools, the Hitler Youth, and parents, resulting in different perspectives on implementing educational plans, which is very inconsistent with educational principles.

Minister's Proposal 197

German Education Minister Rustling believes that this inconsistent and deformed educational method is very detrimental to young people, so he resolutely improved the proposed plan to be simple and easy to implement. He changed the weekly coursework into three sections: from Monday to Friday for school lessons, and Saturday as a school holiday, purely for Hitler Youth training, gathering male and female students together to travel to the countryside further away from the city, seeking a natural life and thereby exercising the body. Sunday is entirely for family life. Since its implementation, education has been unified and the results have been remarkable.

Extending Summer Vacation 198

Not only that, but Rustling also stipulated a simple and effective method for training, which is to shorten the autumn and winter vacations and extend the summer vacation to five school terms. During this period, all teachers must receive considerable new education training. Every summer, teachers, regardless of age, must join cooperation groups to jointly study various issues related to the spirit and physical aspects of the new German citizens, so as to provide the new knowledge gained to the youth they approach, striving to achieve the goal of being role models for young people.

Examining Teachers 199

Rustling's most pertinent statement quotes doctors, who diligently study new treatment methods for patients. In the future, teachers should also continuously and tirelessly study the implementation of education, and should not assume that they have achieved great success after passing the national teaching examination and no longer seek further study. The mission of the cooperation group focuses on testing teachers' abilities and knowledge to guide young people, to see if they can truly handle the job. If teachers do not achieve satisfactory results in the Saturday cooperation group, their teaching qualifications will be revoked. From this emphasis on education, one can see a glimpse of the overall situation.

Eleven Counties in Zhejiang's Tai and Yan Prefectures Request Disaster Relief for Education Expenses 200

The Zhejiang Provincial Ninth School District Guidance Conference held its seventh Guidance Conference and the second meeting of the Executive Committee at the Yanzhong Affiliated Elementary School. Zhang Lingti, Chairman of Yanzhong Affiliated Elementary School, presided over the meeting and passed many proposals. The most important one was the proposal on how to provide disaster relief for education funds in the province's school district. It was decided to send a telegram to the Education Department for disaster relief. The original telegram is as follows: To the esteemed Education Department of Zhejiang Province, Hangzhou. We have investigated that the education funds in six counties, including Jiande, in the province's Ninth School District have always been exhausted. Since the beginning of summer this year, there has been no rain for three months, and the disaster situation is extremely serious. The rural economy has completely collapsed, tax sources have almost been cut off, and it is difficult to collect school rent. The directors of the education bureaus in each county have already been left with more heart than power, and the education cause is about to come to a standstill. Our office, witnessing this tragic situation, dares not remain silent. Therefore, we convened an executive meeting on the date of this document and decided to ask the Education Department to provide disaster relief. For this reason, we specifically telegraph to earnestly request the Education Department to quickly provide disaster relief to help us through this difficult time. The education system will be very fortunate, and the region will be very fortunate.

Another report states that the directors of the education bureaus of six counties, including the former Tai and Zeng Huang, held a meeting at Haimen Taizhou Middle School to discuss how to provide emergency relief for the shortage of more than 160,000 yuan in education expenses. It was decided to submit the above-mentioned shortage amount to the Provincial Government's Finance and Education Departments to allocate funds from local public bonds and tobacco and alcohol license tax stamp duties. It was also decided that the directors of the education bureaus of each county would go to the province by car from Tiantai on the 16th to request assistance from the authorities.

Zhejiang Education Department Orders and Promulgates New Student Movement Implementation Plan for Middle School Students 201

The Zhejiang Education Department, in order to train students in each school, should use the implementation of the New Life Movement as a standard, specially ordered and promulgated the following implementation plan and ordered all schools to comply. The following is an excerpt from the original document: (A) Implementation Principles: (1) Each school should use the implementation of the New Life Movement as a standard for training students. (2) Each school should implement the New Life Movement to enable students to express propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame in their daily lives, clothing, food, and actions, so that spiritual life and material life are combined into one. (B) Implementation Methods: (1) New Life training should be implemented from the following two aspects: A. Public training, with four items omitted. B. Individual training, with five items. (C) Examples of New Life Standards for Students, with thirteen items and one hundred and ten sub-items. Note: Each school should formulate implementation measures for the New Life Movement based on this plan and submit them to the Education Department for record and implementation.

Chinese Education Society Enriches Internal Organization 202

The Chinese Education Society has been established for more than a year. Because the membership qualifications are very strict and the introductions and selections are very precise, only more than 300 members have been absorbed so far. More than 20 branch societies have been established in various places, and they are studying matters that should be promoted and reformed in education. The society's affairs are quite developed. Recently, it was heard that in order to enrich the internal organization, in addition to having each director and alternate director voluntarily become permanent individual members to promote this, they also increased the number of provincial and municipal education departments and universities as group members. They have already received enthusiastic replies agreeing to join. The society has now revised the group membership fees at the third board meeting to be (1) 200 yuan for a one-time payment, and (2) 50 yuan for an annual payment. Members can choose one of the two.

In addition, according to the suggestion of the Anqing branch, the society will contact the former China Education Improvement Society to use the books, address, and funds stored by the society in Beiping. It was also decided to invite five members, including Jiang Menglin, Zhang Boling, Chang Daozhi, Yang Chuan, and Tao Zhihang, to negotiate the acquisition.

Education Department Supervisor Zhong Reduces Inspection Area Due to Eye Disease 203

Inspects Ping and Ji provinces this year, and will inspect Shandong Province next year

Zhong Daozan, Supervisor and Section Chief of the Education Department, went to Beiping to inspect vocational education. Due to the hardships of travel, he suffered from an eye disease (sudden dilation of the pupil) upon arrival in Beiping and moved into Tongren Hospital. Cha Yuan, Director of the Beiping Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, telegraphed the Education Department to explain everything (the treatment and operation by the doctor were successful, but he still needs to recuperate). The Education Department also telegraphed Liu Mingquan, an employee of the Education Department's archive storage office in Beiping, instructing him to take care of him nearby. Yesterday, Mr. Mingquan telegraphed on behalf of the Education Department, briefly stating that Supervisor Zhong instructed that due to his eye disease, he had to reduce the inspection area and planned to complete the inspection of vocational education in Beiping and Hebei first, and return to the Education Department at the end of next month. Regarding vocational education in Shandong Province, he plans to inspect it next year.

The Outlets for Graduates of Yangzhou High School 204

Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou High School has always enjoyed a good reputation. The outlets for its graduates are of great interest to the general public. It has been discovered that the statistics for the ordinary graduates of the school this year are as follows: Five people were admitted to the Tianchu Han Education Foundation (more than 100 middle school students across the country applied, and a total of 10 were selected, with the school accounting for half of them). Two people were admitted to the Liang Shiyi Scholarship, one person was admitted to the Wang Boyuan Scholarship, 19 people were admitted to National Central University, 18 people were admitted to Tsinghua University, 15 people were admitted to Shanghai Jiaotong University, 11 people were admitted to the Central Political School, 5 people were admitted to Peking University, 4 people were admitted to Wuhan University, 4 people were admitted to Beiping Normal University, and 2 people were admitted to Zhejiang University. In addition, one person each was admitted to Jinling, Shandong, Shanghai Business College, and Merchant Marine schools. Two people were admitted to Shanghai Bank. All of this year's graduates have gone on to further education. Among the 64 ordinary graduates of the school last year, only one failed to graduate. This year, among the 78 graduates, only one failed to graduate because he scored more than 50 points in the geography subject. Therefore, the school's performance is ranked first in the province. In addition, all 23 graduates of the civil engineering department this year have not gone on to further education or been unemployed, but have all served in the engineering field. Fourteen people serve in engineering institutions in the province, and nine people serve in engineering institutions in other provinces. Various parties are still competing to hire them, and there is a great shortage of supply. In addition, all the normal school graduates this year have taken elementary school teaching positions. Among them, nine people applied for elementary school teachers in Nanjing City, and eight were admitted. It is heard that the total number of applicants was more than 360, and only 18 were admitted in total, while 8 out of 9 applicants from the school were admitted, almost half of the total number of admissions. In addition, the school's junior high school graduates participated in the provincial ordinary department, grade statistics entrance examination this year. According to the Education Department's statistics, its performance is also the best in the province.

Special Article

Answering Mr. Liu Yizheng for "Wonderful Plan to Protect the Nose" (1) Zhu Yixin 214

Not long ago, I compiled a set of elementary school Chinese textbooks for the World Book Bureau. In the first volume, lessons six and seven selected "Wonderful Plan to Protect the Nose." The original text is as follows:

In ancient times, there was a king who was very tyrannical. One day, he was going to pass through a certain city. The people in the city got the news and were very panicked, because if the king entered the city, the food and drink of his retinue would have to be supplied by them. If the king saw anything they loved, he would take it away. So they gathered the masses to discuss how to prevent the king from entering the city.

A clever man suggested, "We should cut down the big trees in the forest and place the tree trunks and branches across the road to prevent the king from entering the city." When the crowd heard this, they all clapped their hands in approval. Soon, they blocked all the roads around the city with wood.

The king wanted to enter the city, but seeing that all the roads, big and small, were impassable, he had to change his route. Before leaving, he said to a villager, "Go and tell the people in the city that sooner or later I will send troops into the city and cut off their noses."

The villager immediately rushed to the city and reported what the king said. The people in the city panicked again. They immediately gathered all the old and young people in the city to discuss how to protect their noses.

During the meeting, everyone discussed for a long time but had no plan. Just as they were at a loss, a young man said, "Since we used wisdom to prevent the king from entering the city, we should also use wisdom to protect our noses. I think when the king sends troops, he will first capture the clever people, so we only need to pretend to be fools." Everyone thought it was a good idea, so they decided to pretend to be fools and do foolish things.

The king returned to the palace feeling very unhappy. He immediately sent a team of strong soldiers on fast horses to the city to carry out his orders.

The soldiers arrived outside the city and saw several old men carrying stones to the mountains. The officer reined in his horse and asked, "What are you doing carrying stones to the mountains?" They said, "We are making the mountain higher so that the sun will rise earlier." The officer laughed and said, "You fools, the time of sunrise is entirely controlled by nature and doesn't require you to think about it." The old men did not believe the officer and continued to carry stones without stopping. (To be continued)

Municipal Education Bureau to Hold 5,000-Meter Race Walking Competition 219

To be Held in the City Center on the 28th of this Month

Registration Open at the Municipal First Sports Field Starting Today

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau announced yesterday that, in order to promote physical education among citizens and to make citizens aware of the Great Shanghai Construction Plan, the First Race Walking Meet will be held in the city center at 9:00 AM on October 28th. Preparations are now complete. Registration will begin on the 19th of last month and close on October 25th. The registration location is the Municipal First Public Sports Field on Daji Road. The regulations for the race walking meet have been submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and are hereby promulgated. Enclosed is a copy of the regulations for your information. This announcement.

Race Walking Meet Regulations 220

Article 1: The purpose of this meet is to promote physical education among all citizens. Article 2: Any male citizen of this city who is over 18 years old, except those whose profession is sports, may participate in the competition. Article 3: The race walking route for this meet is as follows: starting from the front of the Municipal Government Building in the city center, heading west on Fuxi Nei Road, Sanmin Road, heading south on Songhu Road, heading east on Zheng Tong Road, Fu Nan Road, heading north on Fu Nan Zuo Road, Fu Dong Nei Road, Fu Qian Zuo Road, heading west on Fu Nei Dong Road, and ending at the front of the Municipal Government Building, totaling 5,000 meters. Article 4: This meet will be held on October 28th at 9:00 AM. Article 5: In addition to the Mayor serving as the President of the meet and the Director of the Education Bureau serving as the Vice President, there will be a Secretary-General and a Chief Referee, as well as several judges and staff members, who will be appointed by the Director of the Education Bureau. Article 6: All athletes must follow the route designated by the meet completely and move forward. If they go the wrong route, they should return to the original wrong spot and start again. They must not step onto the sidewalk, or ask for assistance, or obstruct other athletes from advancing. Article 7: Athletes may not request guides. Article 8: The standard for selecting winning athletes will be 15% of the participants. Article 9: The competition matters shall be presided over by the chief referee. The athletes shall not protest the judgment of the chief referee. Article 10: These regulations shall be implemented upon approval and promulgation by the Municipal Education Bureau and the Municipal Government.

Spring and Autumn

Little Western Paradise 228

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 3: Eternally Relieving Suffering, Showing Pity for a Young Girl at the Door; Hearing of Hardships, Cherishing Heaven, Visiting a Home

The teahouse attendant said: When people reach the point of selling their sons and daughters, they prioritize satisfying their hunger first. They can't concern themselves with other things. During the great drought years ago, tens of thousands of women from Shaanxi married into Shanxi. The deal was agreed upon one day, and they left the next. Who could worry about what happened afterward? We only heard that disaster victims got married and left, but we never heard of them returning. Take the young girl who just came, for example. Even if her two generations above were willing to sell her, it wouldn't be easy to find a patron. Cheng Zhiqian said: Her two generations above probably just wanted to find a place to eat, so they'd just casually find a son-in-law. Why would they need to sell this child to someone as a concubine? The teahouse attendant laughed: Mr. Cheng, think about it. Those without money can't afford her; they still have to support two generations. Those with money wouldn't legitimately marry a refugee girl. Cheng Zhiqian nodded, seemingly agreeing with what he said, and slowly paced back and forth under the eaves, pondering the attendant's words. Suddenly, he smiled: I remembered a saying. He turned around to look at the teahouse attendant. The teahouse attendant laughed: Mr. Cheng, if you want this girl, it's easy to arrange. I can run errands for you. Cheng Zhiqian shook his head repeatedly and laughed: No, no. It's what you said to the girl just now, that there are foreign cave dwellings behind. I don't understand that. Cave dwellings are unique to the Northwest, so how can they be related to the word "foreign"? What kind of style are the foreign cave dwellings you're talking about? The teahouse attendant laughed: Saying they're foreign-style just means the cave dwellings are well-made. There aren't any cave dwellings there. Cheng Zhiqian said: I've visited the cave dwellings all the way from Luoyang to Xi'an. The worst ones are just like animal dens. You can't even stand up straight when you enter. It's pitch black inside. You can touch the dirt on the cave walls. There are all kinds of smells inside, but nothing else. (43)

Eunuchs of the Former Qing Dynasty 229

— Yi Sheng

Do you know what kind of people the eunuchs of the former Qing dynasty were? I'm sure many people will answer: prostitutes, actors, slaves, soldiers, etc. Haha, wrong! In the former Qing dynasty, those qualified to be eunuchs were not ordinary commoners, but Manchu officials. Their eunuch status was absolute and genuine, without any doubt. Originally, they called themselves "eunuchs" in front of the emperor, without anyone else calling them that. They acknowledged it themselves first.

In the "Record of Fragrant Clouds" recently published in this newspaper, it was mentioned that Yuan Shikai, when meeting the Empress Dowager, called himself a "eunuch." A few days later, there was an addendum stating that a certain gentleman had submitted a letter correcting that Han officials should call themselves "subjects," etc. I remember hearing my late father talk about this anecdote when I was about eleven or twelve years old. Now, I can take this opportunity to discuss it. I haven't studied history, so I don't know if this matter is recorded in official history. I don't know if there are any mistakes. I'll ignore those for now.

The Great Qing Code was compiled by Hong Chengchou, a leftover official from the late Ming dynasty. At the beginning of the Qing dynasty, the Qing court greatly valued Hong's talent and wanted to force him to surrender. They used mansions and beauties to soften him. However, Hong refused to submit and later resolved to starve himself to death for his former country, drinking only plain water to quench his thirst. How strange! After half a month of starvation, Hong not only survived but also looked better. He couldn't help but sigh that it was Heaven's will that he couldn't uphold his foolish loyalty! He finally shed tears, bowed to the north to bid farewell to his former lord in Heaven, and surrendered to the Qing court. It turned out that the Qing court learned of Hong's hunger strike and was awed by his loyalty. They were also reluctant to lose his great talent, so they secretly ordered the people serving him to mix ginseng soup into the water he drank, so he didn't die. This little trick allowed him to be fooled greatly!

After Hong Chengchou was ordered to compile the Great Qing Code, he also took the opportunity to play tricks, as if he was intentionally retaliating, and he also fooled the Manchus. He included a clause in the Great Qing Rituals: "Whenever officials have an audience or make a report to the emperor, Manchu officials should call themselves 'eunuchs,' and Han officials should call themselves 'subjects.'" This clearly taught Manchu officials to willingly equate themselves with slaves. Later, some less foolish Manchu officials vaguely realized that this "calling oneself a eunuch" was not very dignified. However, this had already become an ancestral custom, as fixed as iron, and could not be changed!

Now, twenty years after the Qing dynasty abdicated, the deposed emperor, who used to be the master, is unexpectedly being manipulated and enslaved by the Japanese. There is even a group of new and old Manchu and Han servants who are gloatingly acting as eunuchs of eunuchs. This downward trend is something Hong Chengchou could never have anticipated back then!

Tidbits 230

— (Xiong Yu)

Shandong has no tigers, Zhejiang has no wolves, Shandong has no rabbits, and Western Sichuan has no pigeons.

Owls eat their mothers, elaphure eat their fathers, mosquitoes are called white birds, and fireflies are called red birds.

Huge things eat dogs, cuckoos eat mulberries, cats eat lotuses, all of which are recorded in [unclear]; tigers are named Li Er. When tigers eat livestock, they never eat the ears, which is said to be because they avoid their name. Only the [unclear] eats one person, but only lacks one ear. I have been thinking about this to this day and cannot figure out the reason. I record this to provide for the research of biologists.

Dusk 231

— Zhu Shoutong

What a delightful thing! During this bitter rain, a crescent moon emerges from the thin clouds.

The clear and gentle light, like the fingers of a loving mother, caresses the window curtains, caresses the flowers in the vase on the table, slowly approaches and caresses my messy hair, then quietly moves past, caressing everything else. The small building is everywhere, melting into the embrace of nature. I am also intoxicated by it.

Outside the window, a sycamore tree along the street, with a full head of green leaves, sways its branches, as if nodding and smiling. The moonlight reflects the shadow of the tree, spreading all over the window, the floor, and the walls, all covered with natural patterns and colors, sparse and rhythmic, which no one can write to such mystery. The sound of a piano accompanied by the bells of Van Gogh floats into the room from time to time. It must be a Swenade melody, so subtle, so charming, and all the worries are dissipated to who knows where.

The leaves on the branches rustle, and a few tender green autumn insects are blown in by a slight autumn breeze. They fall to the ground and jump around non-stop as if afraid of people. I remember when I had insomnia, I relied on their chirping to pass the long, boring nights. Now that we meet by chance, let's stay in the room with these guests living under someone else's roof and spend this cool autumn night together.

The Modern Attire of the God of Peace 232

— Qiu

Perming Hair 233

— Zhou Zixin

From the bright and sparkling mirror, my withered and thin face is reflected. The hardships of life are clearly symbolized by such a face.

My scattered and unruly hair is about to be tamed by hot tongs heated with an alcohol lamp. It will be divided into batches, smoothed out, and pressed down. Each time the tongs touch my hair, it is a time of oppression. The sound of the hair sizzling is a pitiful whisper that continuously spreads, tensing and trembling all the muscles in my body. Sometimes, the oppression is so strong and severe that even my skin suffers innocent pain.

What a foolish thing this is! My hair is naturally healthy, yet I forcibly and aggressively try to make it beautiful by conforming to an unnatural standard. Why bother? Doesn't natural beauty exist?

This small matter—perming hair—has left me with so much stimulation and enlightenment. It has clearly shown me that in today's world, peace, disarmament, and everything else are nothing more than hypocrisy covered by a mask. The hair, after being forcibly pressed by hot tongs, isn't it as docile and obedient as a lamb? Only the strong can stand on the victorious battle line. I am also secretly reflecting that the countryside has collapsed to such a depressed state, but I am still so indifferent. Isn't this too unpatriotic of me? Perhaps the main reason is that I am too estranged from the countryside.

Poor and Humble Couple 234

— Zhu Jin

Autumn is gradually deepening. The fashionable men and women in the city have all changed into new clothes; especially the young ladies. Some are wearing light yellow short jackets, some are wearing colorful scarves, and the cheongsams with beautiful curves are of course graceful and lovely; while a group of students in short skirts and chubby legs are also full of healthy charm. In Mr. Wu's eyes, he really feels that other people's clothes are too outdated, at least they are old-fashioned clothes that can be sold in a clothing store.

On this day, Mr. Wu finally received his salary, which had been discounted by 20%. In his dry pocket, he carried a crisp five-yuan banknote from the Bank of China, and six silver dollars. The slight clinking sound of the silver dollars shaking made Mr. Wu feel much more energetic. He puffed out his chest and walked on the sidewalk, looking at the women and listening to the wonderfully sung radio, truly feeling boundless joy, floating as if in paradise.

"Hairy crabs for sale, hairy crabs for sale." The gentle voice of the crab seller, and the fist-sized hairy crabs with a bluish-brown color in the small basket, entered Mr. Wu's eyes and ears, and his heart couldn't help but stir.

Crabs are Mr. Wu's favorite food, but he has been separated from them for a long time. On this day, because he had sixteen dollars in his pocket, he wanted to reward himself with a few crabs for a big feast. So he stopped the crab seller and asked him how much they cost per catty.

"Sir, I don't cheat customers; others sell for one dollar for one and a half catties, but for you, sir, I'll give you ten taels per dollar per catty." The high price made Mr. Wu start calculating in his mind. Each crab weighs at least five taels, according to the current market weight of thirteen taels and six mace, it would cost more than one dollar to buy six crabs. If he uses one dollar to buy food, it can last for at least five days. Mr. Wu thought about the food problem, and then about the rent, and about his wife's autumn clothes. Everything, everything, finally suppressed his appetite, and he hurried home.

As soon as Mr. Wu stepped into the door, his wife was busily playing mahjong with his younger sister and two neighbors. In the small living room, a mahjong table and four chairs were placed diagonally, leaving almost no room to move. Mr. Wu felt a slight sense of melancholy in his heart; in such an environment, his wife still wants to play mahjong, it seems too inconsiderate of him. However, when he saw his wife's yellow face and outdated clothes, he felt that it would be too unfeeling not to let his wife enjoy these small pleasures; besides, the mahjong his wife plays is the smallest kind, with a base of one thousand cash.

However, in this noisy environment, Mr. Wu certainly couldn't do anything in the living room; in the room, the light was too dim, and it wasn't even convenient to read. Finally, Mr. Wu lay down on the bed, wanting to take a nap, but because of the rumbling and clattering of the mahjong tiles and the sounds of his wife's laughter and curses, Mr. Wu not only couldn't sleep, but the thoughts in his heart were stirred up like raging waves.

He thought of his former large family, with high halls and large houses, but now he lived in a low house no different from a doorman's room; and after so many years of struggle and hard work, although he could barely maintain his life, not to mention rising to prominence, there was no hope at all. Even to slightly improve his environment seemed beyond his ability. The ambition of his youth to make a grand career completely disappeared.

The rumbling and clattering of the mahjong tiles, one sound after another, entered Mr. Wu's ears, like exploding bombs, really making Mr. Wu's head swell and his heart vexed. So, because of the bad environment, Mr. Wu also hated the low house, and even hated his wife's mischief. The bursts of annoyance made Mr. Wu unable to rest on the bed.

He suddenly sat up and rushed to the living room with a fierce look. The pale face made everyone at the mahjong table stop laughing and silently shuffle the tiles. His wife's face also turned from yellow to pale, frighteningly, which couldn't help but suppress Mr. Wu's anger. When he looked at her old-fashioned clothes again, his heart was pounding, and he couldn't get angry. So he took out all sixteen dollars from his pocket and threw them in front of his wife, and then stepped out the door in a daze. The vast twilight gradually swallowed Mr. Wu's back.

The Misty Records of Imperial Incense 235

— Original by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Chapter 16 The Empress Dowager Arrives Safely in Her Hometown

As soon as we entered the three northeastern provinces, due to the influence of inspiration, it seemed that the air had changed to a different atmosphere from before; looking outside the car again, the scenery of the fields also seemed a little different. However, if you really asked me to point out what the specific differences were, I wouldn't be able to answer! In short, this kind of feeling happens naturally whenever we first enter a strange place. At that time, our train seemed to be running much faster than usual, probably because it had been forced to roll slowly all the way, and it was also a little unhappy itself.

There is a kind of plant in the three northeastern provinces; it is very famous, and perhaps people from all over the world know about it, that is "gaoliang" (sorghum). I had also heard of it for a long time, but had never seen it before; so after leaving Shanhaiguan, whenever I had time, I leaned against the car window and tried my best to look out, but I didn't see any special plants for a long time. Finally, I went to ask the eunuch who was well-versed in botany, and he pointed it out to me with a smile. It turned out that the gaoliang had not yet grown at that time, and was only one or two feet long after sprouting, so when I saw it, I thought it was wheat! It is said that after a few more months, these gaoliang will grow as tall as a person, and its leaves are very dense, and many families grow it; therefore, when they grow up, from Shanhaiguan in the west to the border of Goryeo in the east, this entire area is simply like being covered with a green velvet carpet. When people look down from a higher place, they only see a piece of green, and all the smaller houses, streams, ponds, and other plants are all covered by the gaoliang and cannot be seen at all! Therefore, people in the three northeastern provinces often call that period the period when the "green gauze curtain" rises. (153)

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Not Forgetting National Humiliation at Banquets 248

— Chen

The 14th's newspaper reported that the Shandong Province decided that government officials' banquets would have 18 first-class dishes, named "September 18th," 11 medium-class dishes, named "January 28th," and 8 side dishes, named "May 3rd," reportedly "to show that we do not forget national humiliation."

We recall that in the past year or two, the Northeast was lost, and the borders of North China and other regions were in danger. The people of the whole country were angry that the country would be destroyed without a day, as if mourning their parents. This is because the unworthy descendants of the Yellow Emperor have deeply received the "substantial benefits" of "common language, common race, and co-prosperity," and their pain is so deep and their sorrow is so great. However, many friends who are accustomed to enjoyment feel that this kind of "mourning and vegetarian" atmosphere is too serious, so they shout the slogan of saving the country without forgetting entertainment, saving the country without forgetting... When people's spirits are numb, they are easily changed from entertainment to saving the country, jumping to slogans such as not saving the country, and therefore, after a series of bombings by airplanes and artillery, there are again strings and dances, a sound of joy.

These phenomena illustrate the process of national disasters and humiliations being forgotten by a part of the people. Now, at the time when the gentlemen of the banquet are eating eighteen dishes and eight large bowls, they are strongly reminded by the names of "September 18th," "January 28th," and "May 3rd" to be alert, which is truly admirable. However, it is unknown what the guests who are visiting the high halls taste after trying the "September 18th," "January 28th," and "May 3rd" in the chef's kitchen. I wonder if the "lingering fragrance in the corners of the mouth" is the taste of delicacies from mountains and seas, or the bloody smell of the flesh and blood of compatriots who died for the country in these national humiliations and disasters? It is also unknown whether, when toasting and drinking, they should "not forget" the "national humiliation" because of the name of a banquet, express sorrow for the motherland, or not return until they are drunk? On the one hand, the guests and hosts must be happy, and on the other hand, they must "not forget the national humiliation," which makes the hosts "cry and laugh," and they must be embarrassed!

When the Pyeongsin Railway was opened to traffic, the wooden sandal friends on the dining car treated us with "mutual benefit soup." After receiving it, it was not seen as any "mutual benefit," so how can we expect people who eat "September 18th," "January 28th," and "May 3rd" to "not forget national humiliation" in the midst of drinking and revelry!

Red Smartweed Flowers Wither 249

— Luo Jia

The Yingtou Lake, shrouded in the morning mist, is fascinating. Every day, the bell of the chapel calls back my wandering dreams. I put on my morning gown and welcome the shallow smile of Yingtou Lake. I stroll slowly, using a poet-like attitude, visiting every flower and grass of Yingtou Lake. I have received enough of every frown and smile of Yingtou Lake. Therefore, I am fascinated by the Yingtou Lake, shrouded in the morning green, deeply, deeply.

The early autumn Yingtou Lake is even more fascinating. On the shallow beach near the water, there are clusters of red smartweed flowers. The red smartweed flowers, shrouded in the morning mist, are fascinating, just like the Yingtou Lake, shrouded in the morning mist. The autumn melancholy, dyed on this early autumn Yingtou Lake, is a picture of Jiang Yan. This is a good source of sadness for a young man who has been traumatized. However, this beautiful environment does not allow me, nor does it encourage me, to cry bitterly, but only a faint melancholy, a faint melancholy. I am happy with this faint melancholy and stop the journey of rushing.

The red smartweed flowers on the shallow beach have faded!

As usual, I put on my morning gown and strolled slowly. I am going to bid farewell to the withered red smartweed flowers. However, when I gradually strolled closer to the beach, the rest was the same, without any change. Yingtou Lake was still smiling shallowly, shrouded in the morning mist. The soft branches of the autumn willow were still a touch of faint melancholy. However, beside the red smartweed flowers, there was a girl in purple clothes. The morning breeze fluttered her purple sleeves. Although I only saw her back, this back was like a beautiful woman with a secluded resentment "leaning on the bamboo at sunset," or this was the flower goddess and moon goblin in mythology.

Staring intently at this back as it slowly disappeared, I returned home disappointed. Every day, when I put on my morning gown and strolled slowly, this girl in purple clothes was always standing by the red smartweed flowers. Moreover, I only ever saw her back, and I watched her back slowly disappear every day.

However, on the quiet morning of the second Sabbath, I could no longer see this girl in purple clothes. Moreover, I could never see her again, all the way to today, which is a full five long years!

But when the red smartweed flowers wither, perhaps Yingtou Lake is still smiling shallowly, shrouded in the morning mist, but what about this girl in purple clothes! Is she still unharmed? When I face this cluster of withered red smartweed flowers, I want to bless this girl in purple clothes.

Autumn 250

— Jie Niao

Crows are cawing overhead.

"Damn it!" He took two steps back. Spitting a mouthful of phlegm, he walked forward again.

The autumn sun shone on the road, and many, many legs, trouser legs in suits, trouser legs in long pants... trampled past. He felt dizzy, as if he was the only unemployed person in this big city, dragging himself behind the crowd.

Walking past many of the same roads, the silk shops were flying flags with big discounts. People were going in and out shoulder to shoulder, and big and small packages flashed in front of him. He noticed the broken single shirt on his body, and beads of sweat seeped out from his neck. He lowered his head and looked at his own toes and walked forward.

It was an hour after he left home that he arrived at Yueyou's house.

His friend was not at home, and his friend's wife invited him to the bedroom. His eyes fell to the corner, where a new cradle was placed, and a newborn baby was sleeping. But this bedroom seemed too spacious. He couldn't remember what piece of furniture was missing from the cradle.

"Sit down for a while, Mr. X, he will be back soon."

He stepped back and sat on the bed.

"How long has this child been born?"

"Less than a month."

The child cried, and the mother picked him up from the cradle and teased him. "Call him uncle," and then rocked him downstairs.

He stood up and looked around the bedroom, as if everything was unfamiliar. He took a few steps back and forth, and his toes kept bumping into scattered objects. He remembered to reach into his pocket, but it was empty. He didn't bring a cigarette case. He stepped back and sat on the bed, and caught a glimpse of a box of cigarettes on the pillow. He picked it up, but it was empty, so he threw it away.

He accidentally saw that the clock on the table was already twelve o'clock. He remembered that his wife was waiting for him with an empty pot, so he got up and walked out. His friend's wife appeared at the top of the stairs. The two of them were standing in front of the door.

"Mr. X, sit down for a while, he will be back soon."

"Where did he go?"

"That... I'm afraid he went to see a friend."

The staircase was like lacquer, and he couldn't see anything. It seemed that his friend's wife had stepped back downstairs, and he stepped down step by step.

"Tell him I came to see him when he gets back."

"He'll be back soon, Mr. X. Will you have a meal before you go?"

After seeing him out the back door, he walked away without looking back.

The autumn sun shone on the road, and many, many legs, trouser legs in suits, trouser legs in long pants... trampled past. He felt dizzy, as if he was the only unemployed person in this big city, dragging himself behind the crowd.

When he got home, his wife was waiting at the door. She stepped aside to let him in, and then followed him in.

Page 19

"Nothing...?"

"Went to see a friend!"

They sat in silence. The clock was already ten past one. His wife ran downstairs suddenly, and came back up to give him a letter.

"Just came in the mail."

A bitter smile spread across his face, and he carefully opened the envelope. After reading it, he tore it into pieces and threw it away.

"What is it?"

Without answering, he took out a cigarette from the drawer and smoked it.

His wife bent down to pick up the larger pieces of paper. On them was written...

"...This Saturday... initiate... an excursion to Zhenru, please you... time to gather at the North Station..."

She looked up. Her husband had fallen on the bed.

A Certain Night 251

— Simon

A heavy rain was falling, and a group of people turned into the dance hall. Inside, the jazz music clashed discordantly with the roaring sound of the rain outside the window. Only a thin layer of glass separated the two worlds—heaven and hell.

The fragrance of hair, the lips of mouths, the scent of rouge, semi-nude white organic statues, semi-nude golden organic statues, a moving spring bathing picture.

Indiscriminately chilling, revolving, a limitless exchange of peach-colored passions...

Dance, dance, everyone is pushing someone into the sea. One by one, the gentlemen threw themselves in, like cicada-fish, cicada-fish-like women!

With each piece of music, a branch slipped into each man's embrace, one slipping into that one's side, and another slipping into this one's side.

Dance, dance, we need excitement, they all said so hysterically, saying it while embracing the women's waists and drifting away, floating.

Everyone danced, but the small young writer was left alone guarding the table.

Half-closed eyes, smoking a cigarette, exhaling white misty smoke, fantasizing...

—Taking the harvest of exhausted essence to gamble on fleeting luxury, exchanging it for some temporary false joy. Thinking of the old suffering of not being able to write a single word for a long time, his enthusiasm immediately died down.

Therefore, he quit dancing. However, these places are precisely the barren places for solitary individuals, and in lonely times, his legs instinctively slide towards the edge. Sitting idly is also quite flavorful, calling for a cup of tea, leisurely smoking, watching the line of fruits before him!

For a moment, he would forget his existence and also lose the shadow of loneliness.

The critic returned and encouraged him, and the celebrity returned and also motivated him. Whoever returned said the same thing.

What they said made his heart waver a little.

So he thought. Watching others dance all the time really isn't flavorful enough, damn it, let's have a good time! He also went into the sea. Everyone laughed and said, but he gritted his teeth.

He immediately suffered from an opium den syndrome. Once he entered the sea, he sank to the depths of the water. One after another, he embraced one woman after another. Stepping to the beat, stepping to the slow melody of waltzes. Dancing and dancing as if in a dream.

Before sitting down, he chased after the crashing cymbals and started dancing again. Several people applauded behind him. But while dancing, he gritted his teeth like that, not saying a single word to the women. He was hugging a piece of wood, turning around and around without looking around.

In pain, searching for happiness, ah.

After two o'clock. He felt a little tired. He felt like a deflated ball, without even the strength to breathe. So he walked out the door.

On the night streets, the rain had cleared, and the wind in the late autumn night was strong enough. With a blow, all the warmth on his body disappeared, replaced by a feeling of utter desolation.

Walking out of a volcano, he fell into the ice cave of the human heart.

Autumn at the Six Banyan Temple 252

— Tuoren

Autumn has already arrived in the human world.

Rui, a frail young man, walked step by step towards the Six Banyan Temple against the autumn wind. When he reached the small gate of the temple, he stopped, as if pondering something, standing there in a daze for about ten minutes before taking a big step and walking up the stone steps.

The Six Banyan Temple, this ancient temple of many years, is shrouded in a desolate mood in autumn. The banyan trees have already been dyed a deep yellow, and the fallen leaves are like chicks in the molting season, scattered by the autumn wind. A kind of serene, quiet, and sorrowful scenery is movingly revealed in this ancient temple.

Looking at the tranquil scene before him, his lonely heart was even more melancholy. He sat blankly on the stone bench under the shade of the trees, as if he had lost his soul, and his thin, dark hands stroked his disheveled hair in silence.

Autumn is a pleasant, beautiful, gentle, and lovely season!

The autumn days are so short! The sun has already slipped behind the trees in an instant, and heavy shadows have covered the stone steps of the main hall of the temple. Tourists have gradually become scarce in the quiet temple, and only Rui sits alone in loneliness in this ancient temple.

The golden light of the sun shot out egg-shaped shadows from behind the trees, as if printed on the walls on both sides of the hall gate like colored paper. Rui, with his eyes wide open, stared at it with great absorption, and the events of two years ago floated up in his mind like phantoms.

It was when he and Ming were about to leave that Ming pulled him together to this famous ancient temple. Because both of them felt the loneliness and unease of leaving, they always silently looked at each other on the stone bench. Ming saw the leaf shadows on the wall, tightly held Rui's hand, and spoke.

"Rui, look, how beautiful the leaf shadows are printed on the wall. I'll make an agreement with you first. Let's meet here again at this time two years later! As long as it's an autumn afternoon with leaf shadows on the wall, is that okay?"

"Hmm, two years later? Okay! After you leave this time, I also hope that we can meet here again one day as you said. However, I think things can't be decided like that, right? I might leave here as well."

"In any case, let's make this agreement! That day will always come."

Rui, when he thought of the sentence "That day will always come," his heart felt so sad that he dared not think any further, because today was the agreed-upon day! But Ming never arrived, only he sat alone on the stone bench. He thought in his heart, "Ming made an agreement with me, why did he go to another world?"

The sun had already slipped over the western hemisphere, and the autumn wind at dusk, blowing on his body, was already a bit cold. Rui, however, was still sitting in this quiet temple, like a fallen leaf that had suffered the ravages of the autumn wind, staring blankly at the wall next to the main hall, recalling the circumstances of his friend Ming's death for the revolution. He remained there until everything around him was blurred and the night god had arrived, before he stood up and walked out of the gate of the Six Banyan Temple with heavy steps. But the image of autumn at the Six Banyan Temple was even more deeply imprinted in Rui's mind.

Stupidity and Evil 253

— Written by Shimazaki Toson, translated by Wakagi

Pratin, in Ibsen's memoirs, once said this: "As Flommer said, humans become evil things because they are stupid. But Ibsen said that humans become unbelievably stupid because they are evil."

If the words of the two are compared, it is very strange and interesting, because if we observe the world according to Flommer's view that humans are foolish, then there will be no kind people in the world. However, if we observe from Ibsen's standpoint, then there will be no fools among humans. At the same time, if we move Ibsen's words to the position of moral theory, then there will be nothing in the world more virtuous than humans.

Recommendation of the Special Issue on Modern American Literature 254

— Yan

Since the emergence of new literature in China, it has completely followed the path of Western literature. However, needless to say, young people who love literature, even literary writers, how many of them have specialized research on Western literature? To take a step back, even among those who have considerable research on Western literature, those who have deep and specialized research on the literature of each nation are truly as rare as phoenix feathers and unicorn horns. This is a fact that no one can deny. We young people who love literature, to speak frankly and impolitely, we not only hope that the writers who are working hard in the literary movement on the literary scene will create meaningful and valuable works, but also hope that they will introduce us to some basic and even general knowledge of literature. However, the majority of our famous writers are planning for their own livelihood and the goal of being in the limelight, and they completely disregard our expectations. The "editorial writers" of literary magazines (because they are writers and also editors) are only publishing crudely made works with savage origins in order to attract attention widely. They do not want to find ways to educate us on basic and even general knowledge of literature. And the various books on basic and even general knowledge of literature published by a group of commercialized book editors are so shallow and ridiculous that they cannot be added to. Even our intellectuals are disappointed, let alone the masses who are the target of the efforts of a group of teachers who advocate mass literature education universities. Recently, "Modern" magazine published a "Special Issue on Modern American Literature," which initially gave us a happy and excited feeling on the advertisements. When we bought a copy to read, it was even more satisfying and aroused interest in studying the literature of a nation. The first thing that the "Special Issue on Modern American Literature" gives us is to tell us that those who want to study Western literature and obtain the knowledge necessary for literary cultivation should study the literature of individual nations specifically. This kind of research can not only hope to obtain rich specialized literary knowledge, but also can arouse a strong interest in studying Western literature. The second thing that it gives us is to introduce us to the systematic and literary knowledge of various departments of American literature, so that we can understand what kind of literature American literature is, where its characteristics lie, and what its value is. This kind of understanding, of course, can only give us a concept limited by the editorial space of a magazine, but this concept is already enough for the initial cultivation of young people who love literature.

These are my thoughts after reading the "Special Issue on Modern American Literature." At the same time, several friends who love literature as much as I do also have the same thoughts as mentioned above. Therefore, I believe that the "Special Issue on Modern American Literature" should be recommended to all young comrades who love literature.

Outside the Greenhouse 255

— Chulou

Downtown,

The street is blowing with the early autumn wind. Female office workers, like nimble butterflies, one after another, wearing the fashionable autumn clothes, holding a big book, walk towards their offices.

Capitalists transport all kinds of novel commodities from the golden country, from the Mediterranean, from England, investing huge capital to create a prosperous Shanghai.

However, SEAL has become an indispensable suffix on the advertising windows of shops. Anyway, there are four seasons in a year, and there are cheap prices every season. In addition, there are anniversaries, second anniversaries... The cheap prices cannot be finished.

People are surging like the spring tide, surging. I cannot bear the low air pressure in the crowd, and helplessly look at the sky, but the sky is also crisscrossed with the wind of electric currents.

After turning two or three corners in a row, as if avoiding a fierce wolf, I walked into a secluded and cold street, my mind was a little clearer, I slowed down my pace, looking east and west, but looking for a poem? I ask myself:

Oh! I saw that a new flower shop had opened here.

There is steam on the glass, obviously, this is warm.

Is the warm greenhouse a warm bed for buds? Wandering people, don’t you think of your home? I envy every leaf and bud in the greenhouse, even though it is only tiny and tiny!

The color of the tulip is noble, and she proudly, with plump branches and leaves, supports her smiling face, it should be so charming! Normal temperature air is protecting her.

It seems like I have changed places, otherwise, where would this chaos come from? Oh! I didn't tell you, I saw another tulip, two tulips, three tulips... countless tulips, they are trembling, no, she is dancing, in the charming rhythm.

Shouldn’t this be some dream, I hear their silver zither-like sound? Looking carefully again, indeed, they, not only them, but there are also some men who laugh with joy: "Flower! Everything beautiful in the world is ashamed and bows down under your dazzling light." This voice seems to accompany the music. So the tulip, with her noble yellow, danced and jumped onto the giant's sleeve, pouring her fragrance into that mountain cave full of thorns, no, it's a nostril. The giant doesn't seem to wake up, but at this moment, he has moved, smiling on his mouth, holding the tulip in his palm.

But unexpectedly, the tulip will grow old, and the giant actually threw an old one out the window. There was a sharp cry outside the window. But the giant still picked up new tulip buds and smiled, he said, "With you, everything beautiful in the world is dimmed."...

How can I not be afraid? But somehow, my forehead hit an ice block.

My mind cleared, I was still outside the greenhouse, my head must have touched the glass, and it made a little noise. Fortunately, there was no one in the greenhouse, I had to stagger away.

Amateur Mailbox

Legal View on Leaving the Family 256

Editor:

I am 26 years old this year, a junior high school graduate. I have been working in a yarn factory for twelve years. I am not yet engaged or married. Now, because I am dissatisfied with my family, I plan to leave the family and establish a father-son relationship with someone. However, this matter has not been approved by my parents, and it is my personal initiative. I don't know if it can be done. Now I have several doubts. Please answer them as soon as possible. I would be grateful.

(1) My original residence is in Jiangxi. Is it an obstacle to the law if I want to adopt a person of Zhejiang origin?

(2) Is this matter legally effective because it is my personal initiative and has not been approved by my parents and clan? Do parents and clan have the right to pursue this matter afterwards?

(3) Is there a risk that the clan will have a bad impression of me and cancel my original residence in the

Page 20

Page 21

genealogy?

Respectfully yours, Wang Shi

Editor's Note: Unless there is an overwhelming reason and the absolute impossibility of living together, there seems to be no need to break away from the family, because having lived together for more than 20 years, you should be able to understand each other better than others. If you take the action of breaking away from the family because of an accidental bad impression and other unilateral reasons, there may be a day of regret and pain in the future. I hope Mr. Wang will give this matter careful consideration. The questions you asked are answered below:

(1) The "adopting a son" you mentioned has absolutely nothing to do with region.

(2) Since Mr. Wang is an adult, he can of course act freely within the scope of the law, and no one can interfere, and there is no need to seek the consent of parents or clansmen.

(3) Whether a bad impression is created or not is a matter of human relations and has nothing to do with the law. Whether or not to cancel the genealogy is not a big problem either, because once the adoptive relationship is established, it is cut off from the original clan, so there is no need to cancel it.

Dazhonghua (260)

Zhang Mengfei Ballad 3:00 PM to 4:00 PM

Opening Chapter Su Qin

The world is cold and fickle, it has been said since ancient times. Su Qin failed the imperial examination and returned home. He once traveled and studied with difficulty. He submitted his memorial ten times, but his ambition could not be fulfilled. He was helpless in the face of bad luck and difficult times. Returning home, he was ashamed to face his parents. His wife did not leave the loom and continued to weave. His sister-in-law did not cook for him, as if he were a stranger. His parents were angry and glared at him. The whole family looked down on him. Su Qin was annoyed and ashamed, and had no face to live. He wanted to throw himself into an old well and end his life. Fortunately, his uncle Su Gong was old. He persuaded him with good words and saved him from death. From then on, he studied hard under the window with great determination. He pierced his thigh with an awl and tied his hair to the beam to study deeply. Finally, he persuaded the princes with his eloquent tongue. He united the six kingdoms against the strong Qin. One day, he returned to his hometown. His ambition was high and he was respected. In the end, one must become famous.
